          <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
           <a data-analytics-link="article" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://www.deseret.com/utah/2021/3/20/22295510/steve-jobs-of-the-skies-ready-do-it-again-breeze-david-neeleman-setbacks-adhd-launch-four-airlines">
            Utah’s ‘Steve Jobs of the Skies’ is ready to do it again
           </a>
          </h2>
          <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
           Utah entrepreneur David Neeleman has overcome setbacks and downturns and his own ADHD to launch four different airlines. And now he’s set to launch his fifth.
          </p>
          <div class="c-byline">
           <span class="c-byline-wrapper">

          <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
           <a data-analytics-link="article" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://www.deseret.com/indepth/2021/3/20/22322732/tribes-in-northern-california-yurok-karuk-try-to-close-digital-divide-amid-pandemic">
            How tribes in Northern California are working to close the digital divide
           </a>
          </h2>
          <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
           Tribal governments in Humboldt County, California have become a potential model for other rural areas seeking to give more families broadband access.
          </p>
          <div class="c-byline">
           <span class="c-byline-wrapper">
            By
            <span class="c-byline__item">

              </span>
             </a>
            </span>

           </a>
          </h2>
          <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">

          <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
           <a data-analytics-link="article" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://www.deseret.com/utah/2021/3/20/22285689/diversity-the-workforce-has-become-a-major-goal-for-some-utah-employers-black-chamber-living-color">
            Workforce diversity a major goal for some Utah employers — what’s holding them back?
           </a>
          </h2>
          <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
           As Utah’s minority population grows, Salt Lake area companies are attempting to seize the opportunity to bring more diversity to their workforce and making a concerted effort to retain those employees to enhance their businesses and improve their communities.
          </p>
          <div class="c-byline" data-cdata='{"timestamp":1616298882}' data-cid="site/byline-1616362359_7691_892643">

             and

            </span>
            <span class="c-byline__item">

             <a data-analytics-link="feature" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://www.deseret.com/indepth/2021/3/19/22321484/critics-say-trumps-citizenship-test-was-harder-heres-what-happened-to-the-failure-rate-biden">
              Critics say Trump made the citizenship test harder. Here’s what actually happened to the failure rate
             </a>
            </h2>
            <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
             The Biden administration will revert to a 2008 civics test as it prepares for other changes in the naturalization process.
            </p>

               </span>
               <span class="c-rock-list__entry-blurb">

        var data = { 'Page Title':document.title, 'GA Track Prefix':'t1.', 'geoip_continent': continent[1] };
        var dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
        dataLayer
          .filter(function(m) { return !!m['Network'] })
          .forEach(function(m) {
            Object.keys(m).forEach(function(k) { data[k] = m[k] });
          });

        var userid = data['Logged in Status'];
        data['User ID'] = (typeof userid === 'number') ? userid : null;
        phonographEvents.push(['pageload', data]);
      })();
  </script>
  <!-- End Phonograph -->

})();
  </script>
